                  <hi rend="ital">Information; a piece of information; intelligence; an announcement; news; tidings; a piece of news; an account; a narrative,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">narration; a story:</hi> or <hi rend="ital">what is related from another</hi> or <hi rend="ital">others:</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">خَبَرٌ</foreign>: (S, Msb, K:) it is generally held to be syn. with <foreign lang="ar">خَبَرٌ</foreign>; but accord. to Er-Rághib, signifies <hi rend="ital">an announcement of great utility, from which results either knowledge</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a predominance of opinion, and true:</hi> (TA:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَنْبَآءُ</foreign>. (K.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">النَّبَأُ العَظِيمُ</foreign> [Kur, lxxviii. 2,] accord. to some, <hi rend="ital">The Kur-án:</hi> others say, <hi rend="ital">the resurrection:</hi> and others, <hi rend="ital">the case of the Prophet.</hi> (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">الأَنْبَآءُ</foreign>, in the Kur, xxviii. 66, (<foreign lang="ar">فَعَمِيَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الأَنْبَآءُ</foreign>) signifies <hi rend="ital">The allegations, pleas,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">excuses.</hi> (TA.)    </entryFree>29:T1198,<entryFree id="n39148" key="نَبِىْءٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">نَبِىْءٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, K,) pronounced with <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign> in the dial. of the people of Mekkeh, (S,) whose pronunciation of it is disapproved by Sb on account of its uncommonness; (TA;) by others, <foreign lang="ar">نَبِىٌّ</foreign>, without <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>; (S, K, TA;) <hi rend="ital">A prophet:</hi> (TA:) of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَعِيلٌ</foreign> used in the sense of the measure <foreign lang="ar">مُفْعل</foreign> [i. e. <foreign lang="ar">مُفْعِلٌ</foreign> or <foreign lang="ar">مَفْعَلٌ</foreign>] (IB) or <foreign lang="ar">فَاعِلٌ</foreign> (S, Es-Sunoosee) or <foreign lang="ar">مَفْعُولٌ</foreign>; (Es-Sunoosee) i. e., <hi rend="ital">who acquaints</hi> or <hi rend="ital">informs mankind,</hi> (S, K, TA,) or <hi rend="ital">who is acquainted</hi> or <hi rend="ital">informed, respecting God and things unseen:</hi> or accord. to some, it is derived from <foreign lang="ar">نَبْوَةٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">نَبَاوَةٌ</foreign> signifying “ elevation; ” (see art. <foreign lang="ar">نبو</foreign>;) in which case it is originally without <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>: or, accord. to others, from <foreign lang="ar">نَبِىْءٌ</foreign> in a sense given below; that of “ a conspicuous way. ” (TA.) It is a less special word than <foreign lang="ar">رَسُولٌ</foreign> [when thereby is meant an apostle of God]; for every <foreign lang="ar">رسول</foreign> is a <foreign lang="ar">نبىّ</foreign>, but not every <foreign lang="ar">نبىّ</foreign> is a <foreign lang="ar">رسول</foreign>. (TA.) Pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَنْبِيَآءُ</foreign> (S, K, without <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>, because the <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign> is changed into <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign> in the sing., S,) and <foreign lang="ar">نُبَأٓءُ</foreign> (S, K, like <foreign lang="ar">كُرَمَآءُ</foreign> [pl. of <foreign lang="ar">كَرِيمٌ</foreign>] TA,) and <foreign lang="ar">أَنْبَآءٌ</foreign> [K, these two preserving the original radical <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>] and <foreign lang="ar">نَبِيُّونَ</foreign>, (K,) without <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>: (TA:) but some pronounced the first and last of these pls., in the Kur-án, with <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>; though the more approved pronunciation is without <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>. (TA.) The dim. is <foreign lang="ar">نُبَيّئٌ</foreign>, (S, K,) with those who make the pl. <foreign lang="ar">نُبَأٓءٌ</foreign> [or <foreign lang="ar">أَنْبَآءٌ</foreign>]; but with those who make the pl. <foreign lang="ar">أَنْبِيَآء</foreign>, it is <foreign lang="ar">نُبَىٌّ</foreign>. (K.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  An Arab of the desert said to Mohammad, <foreign lang="ar">يَا نَبِىْءَ اللّٰهِ</foreign>, and the latter disapproved of his pronouncing <foreign lang="ar">نبىء</foreign> in this case with <foreign lang="ar">ء</foreign>, because, as it signifies <hi rend="ital">An emigrant,</hi> he meant thereby to call him an emigrant from Mekkeh to El-Medeeneh. (S, K, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">نَبِىْءٌ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">A conspicuous, an evident,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a clear, way.</hi> (K.) Hence, accord. to some, the apostle [or rather prophet] is so called, because he is the conspicuous, evident, way, that conducts to God. (MF.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">نَبِىْءٌ</foreign> and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n39148-1" target="نَابِئٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n39150"/></foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">An elevated,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a protuberant,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">gibbous, place.</hi> (K.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  Hence it is said in a trad., <foreign lang="ar">لَا تُصَلُّوا عَلَى النَّبِىْءِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Pray not upon the place that is elevated,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">protuberant</hi>].
